=====================================================================
FEDEX FREIGHT ADDITIONAL PICKUP AND DELIVERY CHARGE TIERS BY ZIP CODE
=====================================================================

CONTIGUOUS U.S.
An additional pickup and delivery charge will apply to shipments to/from select contiguous 
U.S. ZIP codes. For a list of the ZIP codes where this charge applies, see below. 
The additional charge applies to shipments rated using FedEx Freight zone-based pricing.

Effective Jan. 7, 2019

FedEx reserves the right in its sole discretion to change, without notice and as frequently 
as it determines, the list of postal codes where a pickup or delivery charge may apply.
